BNWJapanSetup = {
	JAP_Imperial_Court_Setup = yes
	JAPSetUpLegislation = yes
	BNW_Japan_Election_Setup = yes
}
JAP_Imperial_Court_Setup = {
	clear_array = Jyushin_Opinion
	clear_array = Jyushin_Weightage

	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Opinion = 3 } #The Privy Council
	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Opinion = 2 } #The Naidaijin
	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Opinion = 4 } #Imperial Family
	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Opinion = 4 } #Aide-de-camp
	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Opinion = 1 } #Lord Steward

	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Weightage = 20 } #The Privy Council
	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Weightage = 20 } #The Naidaijin
	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Weightage = 30 } #Imperial Family
	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Weightage = 20 } #Aide-de-camp
	add_to_array = { Jyushin_Weightage = 10 } #Lord Steward
	JAP_Determine_Ancestor = yes
}
JAP_Court_Opinion = {
	clr_country_flag = Court_Interested
	clr_country_flag = Court_Reactionary
	clr_country_flag = Court_Liberal
	set_temp_variable = { temp_storage = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
        array = Jyushin_Opinion
        value = v
        index = gus
        if = {
	    	limit = {
	    		check_variable = { v = 2 }
	    	}
	    	add_to_temp_variable = { temp_storage = Jyushin_Weightage^gus }
	    }
    }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { temp_storage > 50 } }
		set_country_flag = Court_Interested
		set_country_flag = Court_Reactionary
	}
	set_temp_variable = { temp_storage = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
        array = Jyushin_Opinion
        value = v
        index = gus
        if = {
	    	limit = {
	    		check_variable = { v = 3 }
	    	}
	    	add_to_temp_variable = { temp_storage = Jyushin_Weightage^gus }
	    }
    }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { temp_storage > 50 } }
		set_country_flag = Court_Interested
		set_country_flag = Court_Reactionary
	}
	set_temp_variable = { temp_storage = 0 }
	for_each_loop = {
        array = Jyushin_Opinion
        value = v
        index = gus
        if = {
	    	limit = {
	    		check_variable = { v = 4 }
	    	}
	    	add_to_temp_variable = { temp_storage = Jyushin_Weightage^gus }
	    }
    }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { temp_storage > 50 } }
		set_country_flag = Court_Interested
		set_country_flag = Court_Liberal
	}
}
JAP_Determine_Ancestor = {
	JAP_Court_Opinion = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Emperor_Interested
			has_country_flag = Policy_Seidan
		}
		set_variable = { Ancestor_Frame = 6 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Emperor_Interested }
			has_country_flag = Court_Interested
			has_country_flag = Policy_Seidan
		}
		set_variable = { Ancestor_Frame = 7 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Emperor_Interested
			has_country_flag = Court_Interested
			OR = {
				AND = {
				    has_country_flag = Emperor_Liberal
				    has_country_flag = Court_Liberal
				}
				AND = {
				    has_country_flag = Emperor_Reactionary
				    has_country_flag = Court_Reactionary					
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { Ancestor_Frame = 4 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Emperor_Interested
			has_country_flag = Court_Interested
			OR = {
				AND = {
				    has_country_flag = Emperor_Liberal
				    has_country_flag = Court_Reactionary
				}
				AND = {
				    has_country_flag = Emperor_Reactionary
				    has_country_flag = Court_Liberal					
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { Ancestor_Frame = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Emperor_Interested }
			has_country_flag = Court_Interested
		}
		set_variable = { Ancestor_Frame = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = Emperor_Interested
			NOT = { has_country_flag = Court_Interested }
		}
		set_variable = { Ancestor_Frame = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = Emperor_Interested
				has_country_flag = Court_Interested
			}
		}
		set_variable = { Ancestor_Frame = 1 }
	}	
}

	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Stage = 2 }
	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Stage = 3 }
	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Stage = 4 }
	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Stage = 5 }

	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Progress = 5 }
	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Progress = 0 }
	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Progress = 0 }
	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Progress = 0 }
	add_to_array = { Nuclear_Progress = 0 }

}

BNWNuclearProgramAdvance = {
    set_variable = { Nuclear_Stage_Frame^Current_Stage = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { Current_Stage = 1 }
	BNWNuclearUpdate = yes
	for_each_loop = {
        array = Nuclear_Progress
        value = nuke_value
        index = amogus

	    clamp_variable = {
	    	var = nuke_value
	    	min = 0
	    	max = 100
	    }
    }
}

BNWNuclearUpdate = {
	for_each_loop = {
        array = Nuclear_Stage
        value = v
        index = amogus
        if = {
	    	limit = {
	    		OR = {
	    		    check_variable = { Current_Stage = v }
	    			check_variable = { Current_Stage > v }
	    		}
	    	}
	    	set_variable = { Nuclear_Stage_Frame^amogus = 1 }
	    }
	    else = {
            set_variable = { Nuclear_Stage_Frame^amogus = 2 }
	    }
    }
	set_temp_variable = { Helper = Selected_Stage }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { Helper = 1 }
	set_variable = { Progress_Displayer = Nuclear_Progress^Helper }
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
}

BNWUpdateCosts = {
	set_variable = { Nuclear_Research_Extra_Cost_True = 0 }
	subtract_from_variable = { Nuclear_Research_Extra_Cost_True = Nuclear_Research_Extra_Cost }
	force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
	set_variable = { Nuclear_Program_Actual_Weekly_Cost = Nuclear_Money_Extra_Cost }
	divide_variable = { Nuclear_Program_Actual_Weekly_Cost = 1000 }
	set_variable = { Research_Cost_Displayer = Nuclear_Research_Extra_Cost }
	multiply_variable = { Research_Cost_Displayer = 100 }
}
BNWNuclearProgramChange = {
	set_temp_variable = { Helper = Current_Stage }
	subtract_from_temp_variable = { Helper = 1 }
	add_to_variable = { Nuclear_Progress^Helper = Temp_Progress }
	#for_each_loop = {
    #    array = Nuclear_Progress
    #    value = nuke_value
    #    index = amogus
	#    clamp_variable = {
	#    	var = nuke_value
	#    	min = 0
	#    	max = 100
	#    }
    #}
    clamp_variable = {
    	var = Nuclear_Progress^Helper
    	min = 0
    	max = 100
    }
	BNWNuclearUpdate = yes
}

OMS_World_Morbing = {
	every_state = {
		limit = { NOT = { is_controlled_by = BHU } }
        remove_building = {
            type = air_base
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = radar_station
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = nuclear_reactor
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = rocket_site
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = fuel_silo
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = dockyard
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = infrastructure
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = hospitals
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = schools
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = prisons
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = offices
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = enrichment_plant
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = missile_silo
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = synthetic_refinery
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = barracks
            level = 10
        }
        remove_building = {
            type = thermoelectric_plant
            level = 10
        }
        set_building_level = {
            type = supply_node
            level = 0
            province = {
                all_provinces = yes
            }
        }
        set_building_level = {
            type = bunker
            level = 0
            province = {
                all_provinces = yes
            }
        }
        damage_building = {
            type = rail_way
            damage = 5
		}
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = { is_coastal = yes } 
	    set_building_level = {
            type = coastal_bunker
            level = 0
            province = {
                all_provinces = yes
            }
        }
        set_building_level = {
            type = naval_base
            level = 0
            province = {
                all_provinces = yes
            }
        }
	}
    BNW_Totalenkrieg_on_VPs = yes
}

QINSetupMapMode = {
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_owned_by = QIN
		}
		set_variable = { THIS.china = 1 }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			is_owned_by = XIK
		}
		set_variable = { THIS.china = 2 }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
			    is_owned_by = TIB
				is_owned_by = MON
				AND = {
					state = 329
					NOT = {
			            is_owned_by = JAP
						is_owned_by = CHI
				        is_owned_by = GAN
				        is_owned_by = SIC
				        is_owned_by = GUZ
				        is_owned_by = GUX
				        is_owned_by = GNG
				        is_owned_by = SHX
				        is_owned_by = MAN
				        is_owned_by = MEN						
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { THIS.china = 3 }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
			    is_owned_by = XIN
				is_owned_by = GAN
				is_owned_by = SIC
				is_owned_by = GUZ
				is_owned_by = GUX
				is_owned_by = GNG
				is_owned_by = SHX
				is_owned_by = MAN
				is_owned_by = MEN
				AND = {
					is_owned_by = JAP
					OR = {
					    is_core_of = CHI
					    is_core_of = GNG
					    is_core_of = MAN
					}
				}
			}
		}
		set_variable = { THIS.china = 4 }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
			    is_owned_by = CHI
			}
		}
		set_variable = { THIS.china = 5 }
	}
	every_state = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
			    is_owned_by = YUN
				has_global_flag = YUN_CDL_Victory
			}
		}
		set_variable = { THIS.china = 6 }
	}
}

QINAddSlotEffect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { State_View = 0 }
		}
	    every_owned_state = {
	    	limit = {
	    		OR = {
	    			state = 604
	    			state = 906
					state = 2429
	    		}
	    	}
	    	add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
	    }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { State_View = 1 }
		}
	    every_owned_state = {
	    	limit = {
	    		OR = {
	    			state = 601
	    		}
	    	}
	    	add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
	    }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { State_View = 2 }
		}
	    every_owned_state = {

    	var = QIN_party_Cap^Politics_Index
    	min = 0
    	max = 100

    	var = QIN_party_opinions^Politics_Index
    	min = 0
    	max = QIN_party_Cap^Politics_Index
    }

QINRegisterLegislation = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { pending_legislation_id = legislation_id^parties_idx }
		}
		clear_variable = pending_legislation_id
	}
	else = {
	    set_variable = { pending_legislation_id = legislation_id^parties_idx }
	}
}
QINRegisterPastLegislation = {
	set_variable = { pending_legislation_past_id = legislation_past_id^parties_idx }
}

QINGenerateBillSupport = {
	set_variable = { Support_Base = -15 } # Base Reluctance.
    QINLegislationOutlookModifier = yes # +10 for aligning legislation outlook, -10 for opposing outlook.
    QINRegimeOutlookModifier = yes # +5 For favoured regime outlook, -5 for opposing regime outlook, no effect if neutral.
    QINConstitutionalityModifier = yes # +2 For every level of constitutionality.
	QINProposalModifier = yes # +5 For proposed by own faction.
	QINStabilityModifier = yes # +1 for every 10% Government Stability.
	QINRegimeTypeModifier = yes # +5 for United Front, other regime types TBA
	QINPartySupportModifier = yes # +1 for every 10% Support
	QINInteractionResult = yes # Decides outcome
}

QINLegislationOutlookModifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
			    check_variable = { legislation_outlook^pending_legislation_id = 0 }
			    OR = {
			    	check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 0 }
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 7 }
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 8 }
			    }
		    } 
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { Support_Base = 10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
			    check_variable = { legislation_outlook^pending_legislation_id = 1 }
			    OR = {
			    	check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 0 }
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 8 }
			    }
		    } 
		}
        subtract_from_variable = { Support_Base = 10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
			    check_variable = { legislation_outlook^pending_legislation_id = 2 }
			    OR = {
			    	check_variable = { opposition_int_id < 6 }
			    }
		    }    
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { Support_Base = 10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
			    check_variable = { legislation_outlook^pending_legislation_id = 8 }
			    OR = {
			    	check_variable = { opposition_int_id < 6 }
			    }
		    } 
		}
        add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
			    check_variable = { legislation_outlook^pending_legislation_id = 1 }
				NOT = {
			        OR = {
			        	check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 0 }
						check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 8 }
			        }
				}
		    } 
		}
		add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
			    check_variable = { legislation_outlook^pending_legislation_id = 2 }
			    OR = {
			    	check_variable = { opposition_int_id < 6 }
			    }
		    }
		}
        add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 10 }
	}
}
QINRegimeOutlookModifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
            	check_variable = {
            	    var = QIN_outlook^0
            	    value = QIN_outlook^1
            	    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
                check_variable = {
            	    var = QIN_outlook^0
            	    value = QIN_outlook^2
            	    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 8 }
				}				
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
            	check_variable = {
            	    var = QIN_outlook^2
            	    value = QIN_outlook^0
            	    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
                check_variable = {
            	    var = QIN_outlook^2
            	    value = QIN_outlook^1
            	    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id < 6 }
				}					
			}
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
            	check_variable = {
            	    var = QIN_outlook^0
            	    value = QIN_outlook^1
            	    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
                check_variable = {
            	    var = QIN_outlook^0
            	    value = QIN_outlook^2
            	    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id < 6 }
				}				
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
            	check_variable = {
            	    var = QIN_outlook^2
            	    value = QIN_outlook^0
            	    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
                check_variable = {
            	    var = QIN_outlook^2
            	    value = QIN_outlook^1
            	    compare = greater_than_or_equals
                }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id > 6 }
				}					
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
}
QINConstitutionalityModifier = {
    set_temp_variable = { constitutionality_influence = legislation_constitutionality^pending_legislation_id }
	multiply_temp_variable = { constitutionality_influence = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { Support_Base = constitutionality_influence }
}
QINProposalModifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { legislation_proposer^pending_legislation_id = 0 }
				OR = {
				    check_variable = { 
						var = opposition_int_id 
						value = 4 
						compare = less_than_or_equals
					}			
				}
		    }
		}
		add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { legislation_proposer^pending_legislation_id = 1 }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 3 }		
				    check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 4 }	
					check_variable = { opposition_int_id = 5 }				
				}
		    }
		}
		add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { legislation_proposer^pending_legislation_id = 2 }
				OR = {
					check_variable = { 
						var = opposition_int_id 
						value = 4 
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}						
				}
		    }
		}
		add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
}
QINStabilityModifier = {
	set_temp_variable = { Stability_Factor = QIN_Regime_Stability }
	divide_temp_variable = { Stability_Factor = 10 }
	add_to_variable = { Support_Base = Stability_Factor }
}
QINRegimeTypeModifier = {
    if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
			    check_variable = { QIN_party_status^0 = 2 }
			    check_variable = { QIN_party_status^1 = 2 }
				check_variable = { QIN_party_status^2 = 2 }
				check_variable = { QIN_party_status^3 = 2 }
				check_variable = { QIN_party_status^4 = 2 }
				check_variable = { QIN_party_status^5 = 2 }
				check_variable = { QIN_party_status^6 = 2 }
				check_variable = { QIN_party_status^7 = 2 }
				check_variable = { QIN_party_status^8 = 2 }
			}			
		}
		add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	}
}
QINPartySupportModifier = {
	set_temp_variable = { sanae = opposition_int_id^parties_idx }
	set_temp_variable = { cirno = QIN_party_opinions^sanae }
	divide_temp_variable = { cirno = 2 }
	add_to_variable = { Support_Base = 5 }
	round_variable = Support_Base
}


QINInteractionResult = {
    if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Support_Base > 0 }
		}
		QINSuccessful_Interaction = yes
		QINSetUPLegislationSupport = yes
	}
    else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Support_Base < 1 }
		}
		QINFailed_Interaction = yes
		QINSetUPLegislationSupport = yes
	}
}
QINSuccessful_Interaction = {
	find_highest_in_array = { array = legislation_log_id index = high_i value = high_v }
	add_to_temp_variable = { high_v = 1 }
	add_to_array = { legislation_log_id = high_v }
	add_to_array = { Legislation_Log_Initiator = 0 }
	add_to_array = { Legislation_Log_Target = opposition_int_id }

	add_to_array = { Legislation_Log_Type = 1 }

}
QINFailed_Interaction = {
	find_highest_in_array = { array = legislation_log_id index = high_i value = high_v }
	add_to_temp_variable = { high_v = 1 }
	add_to_array = { legislation_log_id = high_v }
	add_to_array = { Legislation_Log_Initiator = 0 }
	add_to_array = { Legislation_Log_Target = opposition_int_id }

	add_to_array = { Legislation_Log_Type = 2 }
}

QINSetUPLegislationSupport = {
	set_variable = { QIN_Second_Reading_Support = 0 }
	clear_array = qt1
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^0 }
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^1 }
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^2 }
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^3 }
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^4 }
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^5 }
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^6 }
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^7 }
	add_to_array = { qt1 = QIN_party_opinions^8 }
	
	for_each_loop = {
		array = qt1
		index = parties_idx

		divide_variable = { qt1^parties_idx = 100 }
		multiply_variable = { qt1^parties_idx = QIN_party_seats^parties_idx }

		add_to_variable = { QIN_Second_Reading_Support = qt1^parties_idx }
         
	}
    round_variable = QIN_Second_Reading_Support
	clamp_variable = {
		var = QIN_Second_Reading_Support
		min = 0
		max = QIN_Total_Seats
	}
	set_variable = { Majority = QIN_Total_Seats }
	divide_variable = { Majority = 2 }
	round_variable = Majority
}

QINRegisterImpeachment = {
	set_variable = { Impeached_ID = Politician^parties_idx }
	set_variable = { Impeached_Title = Impeach_Title^parties_idx }
	set_temp_variable = { amorgos = 100 }

	add_to_array = { legislation_id = amorgos }

	add_to_array = { legislation_proposer^amorgos = 1 }

    set_variable = { legislation_constitutionality^amorgos = 3 }
	set_variable = { legislation_type^amorgos = 2 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Politician_Faction^parties_idx < 3 }
		}
	    set_variable = { legislation_outlook^amorgos = 0 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = { Politician_Faction^parties_idx < 3 }
				check_variable = { Politician_Faction^parties_idx > 5 }
			}
		}
	    set_variable = { legislation_outlook^amorgos = 2 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { Politician_Faction^parties_idx < 3 }
				check_variable = { Politician_Faction^parties_idx > 5 }
			}
		}
	    set_variable = { legislation_outlook^amorgos = 1 }		
	}
	add_to_array = { legislation_effect^amorgos = 0 }
	set_variable = { legislation_reading^amorgos = 1 }
	set_variable = { legislation_committee^amorgos = 4 }
}
QINRegisterBudget = {
	set_temp_variable = { amorgos = 101 }

	add_to_array = { legislation_id = amorgos }
	add_to_array = { legislation_proposer^amorgos = 1 }
    set_variable = { legislation_constitutionality^amorgos = 4 }
	set_variable = { legislation_type^amorgos = 1 }
	set_variable = { legislation_outlook^amorgos = 1 }
	add_to_array = { legislation_effect^amorgos = 0 }
	set_variable = { legislation_reading^amorgos = 1 }
	set_variable = { legislation_committee^amorgos = 3 }
}
QINRegisterRepeal = {
	set_temp_variable = { amorgos = 112 }
	
	add_to_array = { legislation_id = amorgos }
	add_to_array = { legislation_proposer^amorgos = 1 }
    set_variable = { legislation_constitutionality^amorgos = 4 }
	set_variable = { legislation_type^amorgos = 5 }
	set_variable = { legislation_outlook^amorgos = 1 }
	add_to_array = { legislation_effect^amorgos = 0 }
	set_variable = { legislation_reading^amorgos = 1 }
	set_variable = { legislation_committee^amorgos = 4 }
	
	set_variable = { repealing_id = pending_legislation_past_id }
	add_to_array = { unable_to_repeal = legislation_past_id^parties_idx }
	clear_variable = pending_legislation_past_id
	set_country_flag = QIN_Repealling_Laws
}
QINControl = {
	set_temp_variable = { orantankbrigade = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Auditing_Focus = 1 }
		}
        randomize_temp_variable = {
        	var = orantankbrigade
        	distribution = binomial
        	min = -5 
        	max = 30 
        }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { orantankbrigade = 10 }
		add_political_power = 200
		add_to_variable = { QIN_Monetary_Health = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Auditing_Focus = 2 }
		}
        randomize_temp_variable = {
        	var = orantankbrigade
        	distribution = binomial
        	min = -15 
        	max = 50 
        }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { orantankbrigade = 15 }
		add_political_power = 200
		subtract_from_variable = { QIN_Monetary_Health = 5 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Auditing_Focus = 3 }
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { orantankbrigade = 5 }
		add_political_power = 50
		add_to_variable = { QIN_Monetary_Health = 10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Auditing_Focus = 4 }
		}
        randomize_temp_variable = {
        	var = orantankbrigade
        	distribution = binomial
        	min = -10 
        	max = 30 
        }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { orantankbrigade = 10 }
		add_political_power = 50
		add_to_variable = { QIN_Monetary_Health = 2 }
	}
    divide_temp_variable = { orantankbrigade = 10000 }
	set_temp_variable = { money_reserves_temp = orantankbrigade }
	econ_money_reserves_change_raw_money = yes
	country_event = { id = tmm.maclique.120 days = 90 }
	clamp_variable = {
	    var = QIN_Monetary_Health
	    min = 0
	    max = 100
    }
}
QINExam = {
	randomize_temp_variable = {
	    var = whatthedogdoin
	    distribution = uniform
	    min = 1
	    max = 2
    }
	set_variable = { lookatmehector = whatthedogdoin }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Examining_Focus = 1 }
		}
        add_to_variable = { QIN_Bureaucrat_Count = 200 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Examining_Focus = 2 }
		}
        TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_really_low = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { lookatmehector = 1 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { QIN_Bureaucrat_Support = 15 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { QIN_Bureaucrat_Support = -10 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Examining_Focus = 3 }
		}
		TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_really_low = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { lookatmehector = 1 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { QIN_Bureaucrat_Count = 50 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = { QIN_Bureaucrat_Count = 50 }
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { Examining_Focus = 4 }
		}
		TNO_improve_admin_efficiency_low = yes
		add_to_variable = { QIN_Bureaucrat_Support = 10 }
	}
	country_event = { id = tmm.maclique.121 days = 30 }
}

QINLegislationReview = {
	set_variable = { QIN_Committee_ID = legislation_committee^pending_legislation_id }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { QIN_committee_ruling^QIN_Committee_ID = legislation_proposer^pending_legislation_id }
		}
		subtract_from_variable = { legislation_constitutionality^pending_legislation_id = 1 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { QIN_committee_ruling^QIN_Committee_ID = 1 }
		}	
		add_political_power = -5
	}
	else = {
		add_to_variable = { legislation_constitutionality^pending_legislation_id = 1 }
	}
}

QINCompleteLegislation = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = QIN_Repealling_Laws }
		}
	    find_lowest_in_array = { 
	        array = legislation_past_id 
	        value = reimu #Not even used lmao
	        index = marisa
        }
	    set_variable = { legislation_past_id^marisa = pending_legislation_id }
	    set_variable = { legislation_past_proposer^pending_legislation_id = legislation_proposer^pending_legislation_id }
	    set_variable = { legislation_past_constitutionality^pending_legislation_id = 0 }
	    set_variable = { legislation_past_type^pending_legislation_id = legislation_type^pending_legislation_id }
	    set_variable = { legislation_past_outlook^pending_legislation_id = legislation_outlook^pending_legislation_id }
	    set_variable = { legislation_past_committee^pending_legislation_id = legislation_committee^pending_legislation_id }
	    set_variable = { legislation_past_reading^pending_legislation_id = 4 }
	    set_variable = { legislation_past_effect^pending_legislation_id = 1 }
        resize_array = {
        	array = legislation_past_id
        	value = 0
        	size = legislation_past_id^num
        }
	    QINFixLegislation = yes
	}
    else_if = {
		limit = {
			has_country_flag = QIN_Repealling_Laws
		}
        for_each_loop = {
            array = legislation_past_id
            value = v
            index = i
            if = {
                limit = { check_variable = { v = repealing_id } }
        		remove_from_array = { legislation_past_id = v }
            }
        }		
		clr_country_flag = QIN_Repealling_Laws
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { legislation_id^num = 1 }
		}
		QINClearLegislationArray = yes
	}
	else = {
	    QINLegislationCore = yes
	}
	clear_variable = pending_legislation_id
}
QINLegislationCore = {
	#Credit to Pina
    for_each_loop = {
        array = legislation_id
        value = v
        index = i
        if = {
            limit = { check_variable = { v = pending_legislation_id } }
    		remove_from_array = { legislation_id = v }
        }
    }
	remove_from_array = { legislation_constitutionality = legislation_constitutionality^pending_legislation_id }
	remove_from_array = { legislation_type = legislation_type^pending_legislation_id }
	remove_from_array = { legislation_proposer = legislation_proposer^pending_legislation_id }
	remove_from_array = { legislation_outlook = legislation_outlook^pending_legislation_id }
	remove_from_array = { legislation_committee = legislation_committee^pending_legislation_id }
	remove_from_array = { legislation_reading = legislation_reading^pending_legislation_id }
	remove_from_array = { legislation_effect = legislation_effect^pending_legislation_id }
}

QINClearLegislationArray = {
	clear_array = legislation_id
	clear_array = legislation_constitutionality
	clear_array = legislation_type
	clear_array = legislation_proposer
	clear_array = legislation_outlook
	clear_array = legislation_committee
	clear_array = legislation_reading
	clear_array = legislation_effect
}
QINSetPastLegislations = {
	QINInitialHistory = yes
	#This part is for solving the peak pdxtard moment where the last array element
	#for whatever fucking reason cannot display.
	QINFixLegislation = yes
}

QINFixLegislation = {
	set_temp_variable = { sussy_baka = legislation_past_id^num }
	add_to_temp_variable = { sussy_baka = 1 }
    resize_array = {
    	array = legislation_Past_id
    	value = 0
    	size = sussy_baka
    }
}

QINStopAdHocMeeting = {
	clr_country_flag = Ad_Hoc_Meeting
	clear_variable = Extra_Days
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = QIN_Legislation_Stage_1
				has_country_flag = QIN_Legislation_Stage_3
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = QIN_Legislation_In_Recess
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { 
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = QIN_Legislation_Stage_2
				has_country_flag = QIN_Legislation_Stage_4
			}			
		}
		clr_country_flag = QIN_Legislation_In_Recess
	}
}

QINCalculateBureaucratPercentage = {
	set_variable = { sekibanki = QIN_Bureaucrat_Count }
	divide_variable = { sekibanki = 1000 }
    divide_variable = { sekibanki = QIN.max_manpower_k }
	multiply_variable = { sekibanki = 100 }
	set_variable = { mystia = sekibanki }
	multiply_variable = { mystia = 100 }
	clamp_variable = {
    	var = mystia
    	min = 0
    	max = 100
    }
}

BNW_Change_Frame = {
	set_variable = { Temp_Frame = JAP_Region_Frame^Temp_Region }
	add_to_variable = { JAP_Region_Frame^Temp_Region = 1 }
	for_each_loop = {
		array = JAP_Region
		value = v
		index = i
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { check_variable = { i = Temp_Region } } }
			set_variable = { JAP_Region_Frame^i = 1 }
		}
	}
	if = { 
		limit = { 
			check_variable = { JAP_Region_Frame^Temp_Region > JAP_Region_Frame_Max^Temp_Region } 
		} 
		set_variable = { JAP_Region_Frame^Temp_Region = 1 }
		set_variable = { JAP_Electoral_District = token:JAP_Election_Placeholder }
		set_variable = { Temp_Region = 0 }
	}
}
